##  <a id="m-xam.plugin.simpleappintro.buttonslideconfig.-ctor_system.string-system.string-system.string-system.string-system.string-system.string-system.string-xamarin.forms.command-system.string-system.string-xamarin.forms.fontattributes-xamarin.forms.fontattributes-system.int32-system.int32___hsdpqw" />  ButtonSlideConfig.ButtonSlideConfig(string, string, string, string, string, string, string, Command, string, string, FontAttributes, FontAttributes, int, int) Constructor ##
<small>Namespace: [Xam.Plugin.SimpleAppIntro](#n-xam.plugin.simpleappintro__22xces)           
Assembly: Xam.Plugin.SimpleAppIntro           
Type: [ButtonSlideConfig](#t-xam.plugin.simpleappintro.buttonslideconfig__8dh1ir)           
Sources: ButtonSlide.cs</small>


Constructor



```csharp
public ButtonSlideConfig(string title, string description, string icon, string backgroundColor, string buttonText, string buttonBackgroundColor, string buttonTextColor = "#FFFFFF", Command buttonCommand = null, string titleTextColor = "#FFFFFF", string descriptionTextColor = "#FFFFFF", FontAttributes titleFontAttributes = 1, FontAttributes descriptionFontAttributes = 0, int titleFontSize = 24, int descriptionFontSize = 16)
```

##  <a id="m-xam.plugin.simpleappintro.simpleappintro.checkvibrate__lhfpsz" />  SimpleAppIntro.CheckVibrate() Method ##
<small>Namespace: [Xam.Plugin.SimpleAppIntro](#n-xam.plugin.simpleappintro__22xces)           
Assembly: Xam.Plugin.SimpleAppIntro           
Type: [SimpleAppIntro](#t-xam.plugin.simpleappintro.simpleappintro__io5so9)

Check if we need to do a vibration



